                const e = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('school_details'));
                e &&

                (this.sclMD = e.schools_metadata),

                this.logoutListener()
              }
              setUserData() {
                this.userData = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('token'))
              }
              getPubNub() {
                return new Promise(
                  (c, i) => (0, o.mG) (
                    this,
                    void 0,
                    void 0,
                    function * () {
                      if (
                        this.loginService.loginStatus() &&
                        this.checkIfEngagementAllowed()
                      ) if (this.pubNub) c(this.pubNub);
                       else {
                        const h = {
                          element: 'script',
                          url: 'https://cdn.pubnub.com/sdk/javascript/pubnub.4.29.9.js',
                          type: 'text/javascript',
                          rel: '',
                          id: 'pubnub'
                        };
                        yield this.globalService.loadScript(h.element, h.url, h.type, h.rel, h.id, h.child),
                        this.getToken().subscribe(
                          r => (0, o.mG) (
                            this,
                            void 0,
                            void 0,
                            function * () {
                              const g = yield this.testService.getCryptoJS();
                              if (r && r.success) {
                                const e = JSON.parse(
                                  g.AES.decrypt(r.token, this.userData.school_id + '_' + this.userData.user_id).toString(g.enc.Utf8)
                                );
                                e ? (
                                  this.pubNub = new PubNub({
                                    publishKey: e.publishKey,
                                    subscribeKey: e.subscribeKey,
                                    uuid: this.userData.user_id + '_' + this.userData.school_id,
                                    authKey: this.userData.user_id + '_' + this.userData.school_id,
                                    keepAlive: !0,
                                    autoNetworkDetection: !0
                                  }),
                                  yield this.addListeners(),
                                  c(this.pubNub)
                                ) : c(!1)
                              } else window.location.pathname.includes('chat') &&
                              this.globalService.commonGrowl.next({
                                time: 3000,
                                severity: 'error',
                                summary: 'Chat initialization failed!',
                                detail: 'Kindly retry after some time'
                              }),
                              c(!1)
                            }
                          )
                        )
                      } else c(!1)
                    }
                  )
                )
              }
              addListeners() {
                return new Promise(
                  (c, i) => {
                    this.pubNub.addListener({
                      message: h => {
                        if (
                          this.currentChannel &&
                          this.currentChannel.channel_id === h.channel ? this.newMessage.next({
                            action: 'message',
                            event: h
                          }) : this.chatLeftPanelEvents.next({
                            action: 'message',
                            event: h
                          }),
                          this.userData.user_id !== h.message.user_id
                        ) {
                          let r = document.createElement('div');
                          r.innerHTML = h.message.message,
                          this.showNotification(
                            h.message.channel_name,
                            h.message.sender + ': ' + r.innerText,
                            h.message.profile_pic,
                            'chat'
                          )
                        }
                      },
                      presence: h => {
                      },
                      signal: h => {
                        this.typingData.next({
                          channelName: h.channel,
                          channelGroup: h.subscription,
                          pubTT: h.timetoken,
                          msg: h.message,
                          publisher: h.publisher
                        })
                      },
                      objects: h => {
                        h &&
                        h.message &&
                        'channel' === h.message.type &&
                        this.chatLeftPanelEvents.next({
                          action: 'channel',
                          event: h
                        })
                      },
                      messageAction: h => {
                        this.currentChannel &&
                        this.currentChannel.channel_id === h.channel &&
                        this.updateMessage.next({
                          action: 'updated',
                          event: h
                        })
                      },
                      file: h => {
                        this.currentChannel &&
                        this.currentChannel.channel_id === h.channel ? this.newMessage.next({
                          action: 'file',
                          event: h
                        }) : this.chatLeftPanelEvents.next({
                          action: 'message',
                          event: h
                        })
                      },
                      status: h => {
                      },
                      membership: h => {
                        if (
                          h &&
                          h.message &&
                          h.message.data &&
                          h.message.data.uuid &&
                          h.message.data.uuid.id === this.userData.user_id + '_' + this.userData.school_id
                        ) {
                          if (
                            'membership' === h.message.type &&
                            ('delete' === h.message.event || 'set' === h.message.event) &&
                            (
                              this.chatLeftPanelEvents.next({
                                action: 'member',
                                type: h.message.event,
                                event: h
                              }),
                              'delete' === h.message.event &&
                              this.subscriptionList &&
                              this.subscriptionList.includes(h.message.data.channel.id)
                            )
                          ) {
                            const r = this.subscriptionList.findIndex(g => g === h.message.data.channel.id);
                            this.subscriptionList.splice(r, 1),
                            this.updateSubscription()
                          }
                          !1 === this.subscriptionList.includes(h.message.data.channel.id) &&
                          'delete' !== h.message.event &&
                          (
                            this.subscriptionList.push(h.message.data.channel.id),
                            this.updateSubscription()
                          )
                        }
                      }
                    }),
                    c(!0)
                  }
                )
              }
              showNotification(c, i, h, r) {
                const g = new Notification(c, {
                  body: i,
                  icon: h,
                  tag: r
                });
                g.onshow = () => {
                  setTimeout(() => {
                    g.close()
                  }, 10000)
                },
                g.onclick = e => {
                  '/chat' !== window.location.pathname &&
                  'chat' === g.tag &&
                  this.router.navigateByUrl('chat')
                }
              }
              getcompanyLogo(c) {
                return this.http.get(
                  'https://autocomplete.clearbit.com/v1/companies/suggest?query=' + c
                )
              }
              getToken() {
                return this.http.post(
                  this.api_url + '/chat/token',
                  {
                    user_id: this.userData.user_id
                  },
                  this.loginService.options(null)
                ).pipe((0, S.K) (this.loginService.handleError.bind(this)))
              }
              removeListeners() {
                this.pubNub.removeListener(this.pubNubListener)
              }
              getChannelGroups() {
                return this.http.post(
                  this.api_url + '/getchannelgroups',
                  {
                    user_id: this.userData.user_id
                  },
                  this.loginService.options(null)
                ).pipe((0, S.K) (this.loginService.handleError.bind(this)))
              }
              getMembersList(c) {
                return this.http.post(
                  this.api_url + '/channel/getmembers',
                  c,
                  this.loginService.options(null)
                ).pipe((0, S.K) (this.loginService.handleError.bind(this)))
              }
              addPubnubSub(c) {
                this.pubNub &&
                c &&
                this.pubNub.subscribe({
                  channels: [
                    c
                  ]
                })
              }
              removePubnubSub(c) {
                this.pubNub &&
                c &&
                this.pubNub.unsubscribe({
                  channels: [
                    c
                  ]
                })
              }
              logoutListener() {
                this.globalService.logoutTrigger.subscribe(() => {
                  this.flushPubNub()
                })
              }
              flushPubNub() {
                this.pubNub &&
                (this.pubNub.unsubscribeAll(), this.pubNub = null)
              }
              getSubscriptionList(c) {
                if (this.pubNub) {
                  const i = {
                    uuid: this.userData.user_id + '_' + this.userData.school_id,
                    include: {
                      channelFields: !0,
                      customFields: !0,
                      customChannelFields: !0
                    }
                  };
                  c &&
                  (i.page = {
                    next: c
                  }),
                  this.pubNub.objects.getMemberships(i).then(

              addGoogleAnalytics() {
                return new Promise(
                  (i, h) => {
                    if (
                      !document.getElementById('google-analytics') &&
                      M.N.g_measurement_id
                    ) {
                      const r = document.createElement('script');
                      r.src = `https://www.googletagmanager.com/gtag/js?id=${ M.N.g_measurement_id }`,
                      r.type = 'text/javascript',
                      r.id = 'google-analytics',
                      document.getElementsByTagName('head') [0].appendChild(r),
                      r.onload = () => {
                        const g = document.createElement('script');
                        g.text = `window.dataLayer = window.dataLayer || [];
              function gtag(){dataLayer.push(arguments);}
              gtag('js', new Date());
              gtag('config', '${ M.N.g_measurement_id }');`,
                        r.append(g),
                        i(!0)
                      },
                      r.onerror = () => {
                        i(!1)
                      }
                    } else i(!0)
                  }
                )
              }
              pathConfigGA() {
                document.getElementById('google-analytics') &&
                M.N.g_measurement_id &&
                window.dataLayer &&
                gtag('config', M.N.g_measurement_id, {
                  page_path: location.pathname
                })
              }
              userConfigGA(i) {
                document.getElementById('google-analytics') &&
                M.N.g_measurement_id &&
                window.dataLayer &&
                gtag('config', M.N.g_measurement_id, {
                  user_id: `student-${ i }`
                })
              }
              eventEmitterGA(i, h) {
                document.getElementById('google-analytics') &&
                M.N.g_measurement_id &&
                window.dataLayer &&
                gtag('event', i, h)
              }
              toggleVisibility() {
                this.sidebarVisibilityChange.next(!1)
              }
              getUserToken() {
                const i = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('token'));

              getUploadStatus(i) {
                switch (i.type) {
                  case t.dt.Sent:
                    return {
                      severity: 'warn',
                      status: 'Upload started'
                    };
                  case t.dt.UploadProgress:
                    return {
                      severity: 'warn',
                      status: `Uploading: (${ Math.round(100 * i.loaded / i.total) }%)`
                    };
                  case t.dt.Response:
                    return {
                      severity: 'success',
                      status: 'Upload completed'
                    };
                  default:
                    return {
                      severity: 'error',
                      status: 'Upload failed!'
                    }
                }
              }

              timezone(i, h) {

                i = new Date(i),

                  i = new Date(i.setHours(i.getHours() + e)),
                  i = new Date(i.setMinutes(i.getMinutes() + a))
                ) : (
                  i = new Date(i.setHours(i.getHours() - e)),
                  i = new Date(i.setMinutes(i.getMinutes() - a))
                ),
                i
              }

              loadScript(i, h, r, g, e, a, n, u, f) {

                    void 0,
                    function * () {

                       else {

                        'link' === i ? (C.href = h, C.rel = 'stylesheet') : 'script' === i &&
                        (C.src = h),
                        n &&
                        (C.defer = n),
                        u &&
                        (C.onload = v(u)),
                        f &&
                        (C.onerror = v(f)),

                        (yield this.loadMathDelimiter()),
                        C.type = r,
                        document.getElementsByTagName('head') [0].appendChild(C),
                        C.onload = () => {
                          if (C.id = e, 'shaka' === e) shaka.polyfill.installAll();
                           else if (a && a.length) {
                            const P = [];
                            a.forEach(
                              x => {
                                P.push(this.loadScript(x.element, x.url, x.type, x.rel, x.id, x.child))
                              }
                            ),
                            Promise.all(P).then(() => {
                              v(!0)
                            })
                          } else v(!0)
                        },
                        C.onerror = () => {
                          p(!1)
                        }
                      }

              handleError(i) {

                  this,

                        h = null
                      }(i && 401 === i.status || 406 === i.status) &&
                      !h &&
                      (
                        401 === i.status &&
                        (
                          this.commonGrowl.next({
                            severity: 'error',

                          }),

                        ),

                        (this.setRedirectionToLogin(), r = yield this.getconfirmation()),
                        r &&
                        (

                            () => {
                              const g = window.location.host;

                              'app.exam.ly' === g ||

                            },
                            1000
                          )
                        ),

                      )
                    }
                    return (0, A._) ('Something bad happened; Please try again later.')
                  }
                )
              }

                            const R = this.copiedText.replace(/\r\n/g, "\n")

                        }

                        this.testData.c_modules.enable_copy_paste && v && (x = v),
                        this.testData.c_modules.enable_copy_paste && !v && (x = this.copiedText)

              detectPresentation() {
                return new Promise(
                  (e, a) => (0, o.mG) (
                    this,
                    void 0,
                    void 0,
                    function * () {
                      try {
                        if (window.PresentationRequest) {
                          const n = new window.PresentationRequest(window.location.href);
                          this.presentationAvailability = yield n.getAvailability(),
                          this.presentationAvailability ? (
                            this.isPresentationChange.next(this.presentationAvailability.value ? 1 : 0),
                            this.testData.client_data.hasExternalMonitor = this.isPresentationChange.getValue(),
                            this.presentationAvailability.onchange = this.presentationHandler.bind(this),
                            e(this.presentationAvailability.value)
                          ) : (
                            this.isPresentationChange.next(2),
                            this.testData.client_data.hasExternalMonitor = 2,
                            e(!1)
                          )
                        } else this.isPresentationChange.next(2),
                        this.testData.client_data.hasExternalMonitor = 2,
                        e(!1)
                      } catch (n) {
                        this.isPresentationChange.next(2),
                        this.testData.client_data.hasExternalMonitor = 2,
                        e(!1)
                      }
                    }
                  )
                )

                var e = new Event('focus', {
                  bubbles: !1,
                  cancelable: !1,
                  composed: !1
                });

              encryptPayload(e, a) {
                return this.getCryptoJSSync().AES.encrypt(JSON.stringify(e), a).toString()
              }
              getCryptoJSSync() {
                if (!this.CryptoJS) throw new Error('CryptoJS is not loaded yet. Call getCryptoJS first.');
                return this.CryptoJS
              }
              generateAESKey(e) {
                if (![128,
                192,
                256].includes(e)) throw new Error('Invalid AES key size. Use 128, 192, or 256 bits.');
                return this.generateHashedKey('aRGgsrzltsGROcVcNneddX8sQW2vP8', e)
              }
              generateHashedKey(e, a) {
                const n = this.getCryptoJSSync();
                return n.MD5(`${ e }_${ a }`).toString(n.enc.Base64).substr(0, a / 4)
              }

              authSDK() {
                return new Promise(
                  (e, a) => {
                    this.http.get(this.api_link + '/getToken', this.httpRequestOptions()).subscribe(
                      n => (0, o.mG) (
                        this,
                        void 0,
                        void 0,
                        function * () {
                          const u = yield this.getCryptoJS();
                          n = JSON.parse(
                            u.AES.decrypt(n.data, this.userData.user_id).toString(u.enc.Utf8)
                          );
                          const f = new Promise(
                            (p, C) => (0, o.mG) (
                              this,
                              void 0,
                              void 0,
                              function * () {
                                if (n && n.c) {
                                  const P = yield this.getAWS();
                                  P.config.correctClockSkew = !0,
                                  P.config.region = A.N.debugger_queue.region,
                                  P.config.credentials = new P.CognitoIdentityCredentials({
                                    IdentityPoolId: n.c.IdentityPoolId,
                                    IdentityId: n.c.IdentityId,
                                    Logins: {
                                      'cognito-identity.amazonaws.com': n.c.Token
                                    }
                                  }),
                                  P.config.credentials.get(x => {
                                    p(!x)
                                  })
                                } else p(!1)
                              }
                            )
                          ),
                          v = new Promise(
                            (p, C) => (0, o.mG) (
                              this,
                              void 0,
                              void 0,
                              function * () {
                                n &&
                                n.f ? (yield this.getFirebase()).auth().signInWithCustomToken(n.f).then(() => {
                                  p(!0)
                                }).catch(x => {
                                  p(!1)
                                }) : p(!1)
                              }
                            )
                          );
                          Promise.all([f,
                          v]).then(p => {
                            e(!(!p[0] || !p[1]))
                          })
                        }
                      ),
                      n => {
                        e(!1)
                      }
                    )
                  }
                )
              }

              getSubmissionLimit() {

                  compile_count: 0,
                  submit_count: 0,

                  submit_total: 0

                this.testData.compile_total &&
                this.testData.compile_total > 0 &&
                (e.compile_total = this.testData.compile_total),
                this.testData &&
                this.testData.submit_total &&
                this.testData.submit_total > 0 &&
                (e.submit_total = this.testData.submit_total),
                this.testData &&
                this.testData.compile_count &&
                this.testData.compile_count > 0 &&
                (e.compile_count = this.testData.compile_count),
                this.testData &&
                this.testData.submit_count &&
                this.testData.submit_count > 0 &&
                (e.submit_count = this.testData.submit_count),

              }

              getBrowserName() {
                return new Promise(
                  (e, a) => {

                    v = parseInt(navigator.appVersion, 10),

                    - 1 != (C = n.indexOf('neo-browser/')) ? (
                      u = 'Neo Browser',

                      (f = f.substring(0, P)),

                    ),

              publicKeyDecryptWithForge(e, a) {
                const n = L.pki.publicKeyFromPem(a),
                u = L.util.decode64(e),
                f = L.util.createBuffer(u, 'raw');
                let C = new L.jsbn.BigInteger(f.toHex(), 16).modPow(n.e, n.n).toString(16);
                const P = Math.ceil(n.n.bitLength() / 8);
                for (; C.length < 2 * P; ) C = '00' + C;
                const x = L.util.hexToBytes(C),
                R = x.indexOf('\x00', 2);
                if ( - 1 === R) throw new Error('Failed to parse PKCS#1 padding');
                return x.slice(R + 1)
              }

                if (e.startsWith('undefined')) return null;
                throw new Error('Input must start with \'true\' or \'false\'')
              }

              estimationHandler(e) {
                const a = {
                  msg: '',
                  severity: 'success'
                };
                switch (e) {
                  case 'lq':
                    a.msg = 'Image quality is poor!',
                    a.severity = 'warn';
                    break;
                  case 'np':
                    a.msg = 'Could not find your face!',
                    a.severity = 'error';
                    break;
                  case 'mp':
                    a.msg = 'May be another person found!',
                    a.severity = 'error';
                    break;
                  case 'd':
                    a.msg = 'You may be distracted or not looking at the screen!',
                    a.severity = 'warn';
                    break;
                  case 'fn-v2':
                    a.msg = 'Verified user not found, some other user attempting the test.',
                    a.severity = 'error'
                }
                return a
              }

              openDatabase(e, a) {

                        },

                          n(f.result)
                        },
                        f.onerror = v => {
                          console.error(`Error opening DB (${ e }):`, v),

                        }
                      }
                    )
                  }
                )
              }

              performDbOperation(e, a, n, u) {
                return (0, o.mG) (
                  this,
                  void 0,
                  void 0,
                  function * () {
                    try {
                      const v = e.transaction(a, n).objectStore(a),
                      p = u(v);
                      return yield new Promise((C, P) => {
                        p.onsuccess = x => C(x.target.result),
                        p.onerror = x => P(x)
                      })
                    } catch (f) {
                      throw console.error(`Error performing DB operation (${ a }):`, f),
                      f
                    }
                  }
                )
              }
              putItemInDB(e, a, n, u) {

              extractComments(e, a) {
                let n = [];
                if (e && 'string' == typeof a) {
                  let u = Object.entries(e);
                  for (const [f,
                  v]of u) switch (f) {
                    case 'singleLine_singleChar':
                      {
                        let p = 0,
                        C = '',
                        P = [],
                        x = 1,
                        R = '';
                        for (const b of a) 0 == p ? b == v ? p = 1 : [
                          '"',
                          '\'',
                          '`'
                        ].includes(b) &&
                        (R = b, p = 5) : 1 == p ? '\n' == b ? (P.push({
                          comment: C,
                          line: x
                        }), C = '', p = 0) : C += b : 5 == p ? b == R ? p = 0 : '\\' == b &&
                        (p = 6) : 6 == p &&
                        (p = 5),
                        '\n' == b &&
                        (x += 1);
                        1 == p &&
                        P.push({
                          comment: C,
                          line: x
                        }),
                        n.push(...P);
                        break
                      }
                    case 'singleLine_doubleChar':
                      {
                        let p = 0,
                        C = '',
                        P = [],
                        x = 1,
                        R = '';
                        for (const b of a) 0 == p ? b == v ? p = 1 : [
                          '"',
                          '\'',
                          '`'
                        ].includes(b) &&
                        (R = b, p = 5) : 1 == p ? p = b == v ? 2 : 0 : 2 == p ? '\n' == b ? (P.push({
                          comment: C,
                          line: x
                        }), C = '', p = 0) : C += b : 5 == p ? b == R ? p = 0 : '\\' == b &&
                        (p = 6) : 6 == p &&
                        (p = 5),
                        '\n' == b &&
                        (x += 1);
                        2 == p &&
                        P.push({
                          comment: C,
                          line: x
                        }),
                        n.push(...P);
                        break
                      }
                    case 'multiLine':
                      {
                        let p = 0,
                        C = '',
                        P = [],
                        x = 1,
                        R = 1,
                        b = '';
                        for (const $ of a) 0 == p ? '/' == $ ? p = 1 : [
                          '"',
                          '\'',
                          '`'
                        ].includes($) &&
                        (b = $, p = 5) : 1 == p ? '*' == $ ? (R = x, p = 3) : p = 0 : 3 == p ? '*' == $ ? p = 4 : C += $ : 4 == p ? '/' == $ ? (P.push({
                          comment: C,
                          line: R
                        }), C = '', p = 0) : (C += '*', '*' != $ && (C += $, p = 3)) : 5 == p ? $ == b ? p = 0 : '\\' == $ &&
                        (p = 6) : 6 == p &&
                        (p = 5),
                        '\n' == $ &&
                        (x += 1);
                        n.push(...P);
                        break
                      }
                    case 'regex':
                      {
                        let C,
                        p = v,
                        P = [];
                        for (; C = p.exec(a); ) {
                          let x = 1;
                          for (let b = 0; b < C.index; b++) '\n' == a[b] &&
                          x++;
                          P.push({
                            comment: C[0],
                            line: x
                          })
                        }
                        n.push(...P);
                        break
                      }
                    default:
                      continue
                  }
                }
                return n
              }
              checkAllInArray(e, a) {
                return a.every(n => e.includes(n))
              }
              checkAnyOneInArray(e, a) {
                return a.some(n => !!e.includes(n))
              }
              checkWLcheck(e, a) {
                return a.every(n => e.includes(n))
              }
              updateEditCount(e) {
                this.testData &&
                this.testData.c_modules &&
                this.testData.c_modules.answer_edit_restrict &&
                (
                  e &&
                  (
                    e.program_submitted_count > 1 ? this.testData.curr_submit_count += 1 : this.testData.curr_submit_count ||
                    (this.testData.curr_submit_count = 0)
                  ),
                  this.testData.max_edit_allowed = this.testData.c_modules.max_edit_count - this.testData.curr_submit_count
                )
              }
              vectorAvg(e, a) {
                return [(e[0] + a[0]) / 2,
                (e[1] + a[1]) / 2]
              }
              vectorSubtract(e, a) {
                return [e[0] - a[0],
                e[1] - a[1]]
              }
              vectorAddition(...e) {
                const a = [
                  0,
                  0
                ];
                for (const n of e) a[0] += n[0],
                a[1] += n[1];
                return a
              }
              vectorMultiply(e, a) {
                return [e[0] * a,
                e[1] * a]
              }
              calcangle(e, a, n) {
                let u = (a[1] - e[1]) / (a[0] - e[0]),
                f = (n[1] - e[1]) / (n[0] - e[0]),
                v = Math.abs((u - f) / (1 + u * f));
                return v = 180 * Math.atan(v) / Math.PI,
                v
              }
              estimatePoseForBlazeFace(e) {
                try {
                  const a = e[2],
                  n = e[4],
                  f = this.vectorAvg(e[5], n),
                  v = this.vectorSubtract(a, f),
                  p = this.vectorMultiply(
                    this.vectorSubtract(n, f),
                    1 / this.BLAZEFACE_CONFIG.MODEL_HEAD_EAR_COORD_X
                  );
                  if (
                    this.calcangle([0,
                    0,
                    0], v, p) < this.BLAZEFACE_CONFIG.minAngleConfidence
                  ) return 'd'
                } catch (a) {
                }
                return 'ok'
              }

              populateData(e, a, n) {
                this.testData.template_data.sections.forEach(
                  v => {
                    const p = {
                      Sections: v.name,
                      Questions: v.Questions,
                      Duration: v.Durations,
                      Marks: Math.round(100 * v.Marks) / 100
                    };
                    (
                      this.testData.c_modules.practise_test ||
                      this.testData.c_modules.disable_timer
                    ) &&
                    (p.Duration = 'Unlimited'),
                    v.Max_Attemptable &&
                    (p.Questions = v.Max_Attemptable + ' out of ' + v.Questions),
                    e[0].value += 1,
                    e[1].value += v.Max_Attemptable ? v.Max_Attemptable : p.Questions,
                    this.setDuration(p, e);
                    let C = [];
                    C.push({
                      label: 'Questions',
                      value: p.Questions
                    }),
                    C.push({
                      label: 'Durations',
                      value: p.Duration
                    }),
                    C.push({
                      label: 'Marks',
                      value: p.Marks
                    });
                    const P = Object.assign(Object.assign({
                    }, p), {
                      sectionArray: C
                    });
                    a.data.push(P),
                    n.push(P)
                  }
                ),
                e[3].value = Math.round(100 * e[3].value) / 100,
                'Unlimited' !== e[2].value &&
                (e[2].value += ' m');
                const u = [
                  {
                    Sections: 'total',
                    Durations: this.getValueByTitle(e, 'Duration'),
                    Questions: this.getValueByTitle(e, 'Questions'),
                    Marks: this.getValueByTitle(e, 'Marks')
                  }
                ],
                f = a.data.map(
                  v => {
                    const {
                      Duration: p
                    }
                    = v,
                    C = (0, o._T) (v, [
                      'Duration'
                    ]);
                    return Object.assign({
                      Durations: p
                    }, C)
                  }
                );
                a.data = [
                  ...f,
                  ...u
                ]
              }
              setDuration(e, a) {
                'Unlimited' !== e.Duration ? a[2].value += 'string' == typeof e.Duration &&
                'Unlimited' !== e.Duration ? Number(e.Duration.substring(0, e.Duration.length - 2)) : e.Duration : a[2].value = 'Unlimited',
                a[3].value += e.Marks,
                'number' == typeof e.Duration &&
                (e.Duration = e.Duration + ' m')
              }
              getValueByTitle(e, a) {
                return e.find(n => n.title === a).value
              }

              constructor(l) {

                this.data = {

              ngOnChanges(l) {

                this.data &&

              }
              show() {
                switch (
                    this.intervalSub &&
                    clearTimeout(this.intervalSub),
                    this.data.severity
                  ) {
                  case 'success':
                    this.data.icon = b.QO8,
                    this.renderer.setStyle(
                      this.growlCardElement.nativeElement,

                this.intervalSub = setTimeout(
                  () => {

              }
